\medskip
\noindent\textbf{Summary of risk stratification.}
\begin{itemize}[nosep]
\item \emph{Zero risk}: Theorems~A--D,\,H, MC2 bar-intrinsic
  construction, all shadow tower results at finite order;
  depend on no preprint.
\item \emph{Low risk (published)}: Quillen equivalence, shadow
  homotopy invariance, convolution identification, no-bifunctor
  obstruction; depend on \cite{RNW19, Val16} (published,
  peer-reviewed).
\item \emph{Moderate risk (single-preprint, isolable)}:
  ambient $D^2 = 0$ and log clutching (\cite{Mok25});
  Heisenberg sewing clause~(i) (\cite{Moriwaki26b});
  $\mathrm{Ch}_\infty$ interpretation (\cite{MS24}).
  In each case the dependency is explicitly isolable and the
  proved core is unaffected.
\item \emph{No proved-theorem risk}: \cite{GZ26},
  \cite{KhanZeng25}, \cite{AMT24}, \cite{Nish26}, \cite{Vic25}
  are cited as motivation, consistency checks, or inputs to
  conjectural programmes only.
\end{itemize}
\end{remark}

\begin{summary}[Three-pillar chain-level synthesis]
\label{sum:three-pillars-chain-level}
\index{three-pillar architecture!chain-level synthesis|textbf}
The three pillars converge into a single concrete chain-level
presentation of the modular deformation theory.  The logarithmic FM
convolution algebra
(Construction~\ref{const:vol1-three-preprints-chain-level}) is the
native object:
\[
{\Definfmod}_{\!\log}(\cA;\, \mathfrak{U})
\;:=\;
\Convinf\!\Bigl(
\cC^{\log\mathrm{FM}}_{\mathrm{mod}},\;
\operatorname{End}_{\mathrm{Ch}_\infty}\!(A^{\mathrm{ch}}_\infty)
\Bigr),
\]
where $A^{\mathrm{ch}}_\infty = \check{C}^\bullet(\mathfrak{U};\cA)$ is
the Malikov--Schechtman homotopy-chiral input (Pillar~A), the
$L_\infty$-structure comes from Robert-Nicoud--Wierstra convolution
(Pillar~B), and the coefficient cooperad
$\cC^{\log\mathrm{FM}}_{\mathrm{mod}}$ is built from chains on
Mok's logarithmic FM spaces (Pillar~C).

The modular bar functor in these coordinates
(Construction~\ref{const:vol1-log-modular-bar-functor}) is a
stable-graph sum with five-component differential
$D^{\log}_{\mathrm{mod}} = d_{\check{C}} + d_{\mathrm{Ch}_\infty}
+ d_{\mathrm{coll}} + d_{\mathrm{sew}} + d_{\mathrm{loop}}$;
the bar-intrinsic MC element $\Theta_\cA$ receives an explicit
graph-sum expansion with log-FM weights
(Construction~\ref{const:vol1-graph-sum-theta-logfm}); and
the clutching law becomes a literal boundary factorisation theorem
on rigid planted-forest strata
(Construction~\ref{const:vol1-clutching-law-logfm}).

The characteristic shadows $\kappa$, $\Delta_\cA$,
$\mathfrak{R}^{\mathrm{mod}}_4$ are successive invariants of the
modular tangent complex
(Construction~\ref{const:vol1-modular-tangent-complex}),
realising the modular characteristic package as a Chern--Weil
theory for factorization algebras.  The weight filtration
(Construction~\ref{const:vol1-weight-filtration}) stratifies the
modular bar functor: tree homotopies and one-loop BV at
weight~$1$; genuine logarithmic modularity beginning at weight~$2$.
Genus~$2$ is the first point where all three shell types
(loop$\circ$loop, sep$\circ$loop, planted-forest) appear together
(Construction~\ref{const:vol1-genus-two-shells}).

The full chain-level architecture comprises the following
identifications proved in
\S\ref{subsec:three-preprints-chain-level}:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\alph*)}]
\item The \emph{graphwise cocomposition}
  $\Delta^{\log}_\Gamma := (\nu_\Gamma)_*\circ
  \operatorname{Res}_{D^{\log}_\Gamma}$ makes the log-FM
  coefficient cooperad explicit
  (Construction~\ref{const:vol1-graphwise-log-fm-cocomposition}),
  and yields graphwise Taylor coefficients $\ell_k^{(g)} =
  \sum_\Gamma |\operatorname{Aut}(\Gamma)|^{-1}\ell_\Gamma$.
\item The \emph{boundary operators} $d_{\mathrm{sew}}$,
  $d_{\mathrm{pf}}$, $\hbar\Delta$ are residue correspondences on
  separating, planted-forest, and non-separating strata respectively
  (Construction~\ref{const:vol1-boundary-operators-residue}).
\item The \emph{rigid planted-forest correction} is the completed
  push--pull sum $d_{\mathrm{pf}} = \sum_\rho \epsilon_\rho\,
  (\kappa_\rho)_* \operatorname{pr}_\rho^* \otimes \mu_\rho$,
  literally Mok's degeneration formula transported into the
  convolution algebra
  (Construction~\ref{const:vol1-rigid-planted-forest-push-pull}).
\item The \emph{MC $\simeq$ twisting data identification}:
  $\operatorname{MC}_\bullet({\Definfmod}_{\!\log}) \simeq
  \operatorname{Tw}_{\alpha^{\mathrm{mod}}}$, and $\Theta_\cA$ is
  the universal modular twisting morphism
  (Corollary~\ref{cor:vol1-theta-log-fm-twisting-data}).
\item The \emph{depth filtration} gives every coefficient of
  $\Theta_\cA$ a tridegree $(g,n,d)$ from Mok's stratification
  (Definition~\ref{def:vol1-rigid-planted-forest-depth-filtration}).
\item The \emph{first two weights} are completely explicit:
  weight~$1$ carries the Malikov--Schechtman Jacobiator homotopy
  and the BV loop operator; genuine logarithmic modularity begins
  at weight~$2$
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:vol1-first-two-weights-log-fm}).
\item The \emph{genus spectral sequence} from the genus filtration
  on the strict modular deformation dg~Lie algebra has
  differentials that are the successive obstruction
  maps~$\operatorname{Ob}_g$
  (Construction~\ref{const:vol1-genus-spectral-sequence}).
\item The \emph{primitive kernel compression}
  (\S\ref{subsec:primitive-kernel-compression}):
  the cofree-coderivation principle reduces the entire stable-graph
  expansion $\Theta_\cA = \sum_\Gamma |\operatorname{Aut}(\Gamma)|^{-1}
  W_\Gamma^{\log\mathrm{FM}}\Phi_\Gamma^\cA$ to a single primitive
  element $\mathfrak{K}_\cA \in \operatorname{Prim}^{\log}_{\mathrm{mod}}(\cA)$
  (Definition~\ref{def:primitive-log-modular-kernel}).  The fundamental
  equivalence $(Q_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}})^2 = 0 \iff d\mathfrak{K}_\cA +
  \mathfrak{K}_\cA \star \mathfrak{K}_\cA +
  \hbar\,\Delta_{\mathrm{ns}}(\mathfrak{K}_\cA) = 0$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:primitive-to-global-reconstruction}) replaces the
  obstruction tower by one structural equation.  Its genus-$2$ and
  genus-$3$ projections give primitive shell equations stratified
  by family regime: Heisenberg (pure loop), affine (loop + bracket),
  Virasoro/$\mathcal{W}_N$ (loop + bracket + rigid)
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:primitive-shell-equations}).
  The finite-rank branch BV packet
  (Definition~\ref{def:reduced-branch-master-action}) carries a
  modular master action $S_\cA^{\mathrm{br}}$ whose QME
  $\hbar\Delta^{\mathrm{br}} S + \frac{1}{2}\{S,S\}_{\mathrm{BV}} = 0$
  is the finite-rank shadow of the primitive MC equation.
  The spectral determinant $\Delta_\cA$ acquires a canonical square
  root $\delta_\cA$ as a metaplectic half-density on the branch
  sector (Corollary~\ref{cor:metaplectic-square-root}).
  The shadow tower is homotopy invariant
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-homotopy-invariance}).
\end{enumerate}

The native end-state of the programme is the chain
\[
\mathfrak{K}_\cA
\;\xrightarrow{\;\operatorname{FT}^{\log}_{\mathrm{mod}}\;}
Q_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}}
\;\xrightarrow{\;\text{branch proj.}\;}
S_\cA^{\mathrm{br}}
\;\xrightarrow{\;\text{half-density}\;}
\delta_\cA,
\]
in which the scalar class $\kappa(\cA)$, the spectral determinant
$\Delta_\cA$, the branch-active quotient, and the nonlinear resonance
classes are successive shadows of one primitive master object
$\mathfrak{K}_\cA$
(\S\ref{subsec:primitive-kernel-compression}).
\end{summary}

\begin{remark}[Design constraint: failure of two-sided bifunctoriality]
\label{rem:no-bifunctor}
\index{bifunctoriality!failure of two-sided}
\index{one-slot obstruction}
Robert-Nicoud--Wierstra~\cite[Section~6]{RNW19} prove that although
the convolution functor $\operatorname{hom}_\alpha(-,-)$ extends to
$\infty_\alpha$-morphisms in either slot separately, there is
\emph{no} honest bifunctor accepting $\infty$-morphisms in both slots
simultaneously.  The consequences:
\begin{itemize}
\item Bar-cobar extends to $\infty$-morphisms of chiral algebras (slot~2)
  and to $\infty$-morphisms of chiral coalgebras (slot~1), but not both
  simultaneously.
\item The MC3 categorical lift
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:categorical-cg-all-types}) proceeds one slot at a
  time.  The prefundamental CG closure
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:prefundamental-clebsch-gordan}) works at the
  character level ($K_0$) precisely because characters live in one slot;
  the categorical lift requires both.
\item Any claim of two-sided functoriality for bulk/boundary/line
  constructions must be replaced by a homotopy-coherent correspondence
  formalism.
\end{itemize}
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[Three-pillar architecture and the MC open problems]
\label{rem:three-pillar-mc-unification}
\index{three-pillar architecture!MC open problems}
\index{MC open problems!three-pillar unification}
The three-pillar architecture determines the MC resolution strategy:
\begin{itemize}
\item \emph{MC1 and MC2}:  Pillar~B realizes every algebra as an MC
  element in the modular convolution $sL_\infty$-algebra; the
  finite-order projections $\Theta_\cA^{\leq r}$ (the proved shadow
  Postnikov tower) are the constructive content.
\item \emph{MC3}:  MC3 is proved for all simple types (Theorem~\ref{thm:categorical-cg-all-types}, Corollary~\ref{cor:mc3-all-types}).  The proof has four components: (i)~categorical CG decomposition at generic spectral parameters, proved via multiplicity-free $\ell$-weights (Chari--Moura~\cite{ChariMoura06}) and block separation in~$\mathcal{O}^{\mathrm{sh}}$; (ii)~shifted-prefundamental generation; (iii)~pro-Weyl recovery; (iv)~Francis--Gaitsgory completion.  Components~(ii)--(iv) are type-independent (Proposition~\ref{prop:mc3-automatic-generalization}).  The type~$A$ proof (Theorem~\ref{thm:mc3-type-a-resolution}) was the original template; the all-types generalization replaces the minuscule hypothesis with the strictly weaker multiplicity-free $\ell$-weight property, which holds universally.  The one-slot obstruction (Remark~\ref{rem:no-bifunctor}) forces a one-slot-at-a-time strategy, which the block-separation argument respects.

  \emph{Strategy by Dynkin type (superseded).}
  The multiplicity-free $\ell$-weight approach
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:categorical-cg-all-types}) gives a
  \emph{uniform} proof for all simple types, bypassing the
  type-specific strategies below.  They are recorded for
  historical context only.
  Types $B_n$, $C_n$, $F_4$: fold from type~$A_{2n-1}$,
  $A_{2n}$, $E_6$ respectively; the type-$A$ theorem descends
  to the fixed-point category under the diagram automorphism.
  Types $D_n$, $E_6$, $E_7$: cluster category
  (Hern\'andez--Leclerc) provides categorical CG via the
  cluster-tilting structure.
  Types $E_8$, $F_4$ (non-folded route): hardest cases,
  potentially requiring Coulomb branch geometry
  (Braverman--Finkelberg--Nakajima).

\begin{construction}[MC3 status by Dynkin type]
\label{constr:mc3-difficulty-gradient-concordance}
\index{MC3!status by type|textbf}
\index{Dynkin type!MC3 status}
\textbf{MC3 is proved for all simple types}
(Corollary~\ref{cor:mc3-all-types}).
Package~(i) (categorical CG) uses multiplicity-free
$q$-characters \cite{FrenkelMukhin01, Nakajima04, ChariMoura06}
transferred to Yangians via~\cite{GTL17}
(Theorem~\ref{thm:categorical-cg-all-types}).
Thick generation of $\mathrm{Rep}_{\mathrm{fd}}$ by evaluation
modules holds for all types
(Corollary~\ref{cor:dk2-thick-generation-all-types}).
Packages~(ii)--(iv) are type-independent
(Proposition~\ref{prop:mc3-automatic-generalization}).
\end{construction}

\item \emph{MC4}:  The formal completion theory is \textbf{proved} by
  the strong completion-tower theorem
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:completed-bar-cobar-strong}): the finite-stage
  bar-cobar duality passes to inverse limits automatically once the
  filtration is strong (arity cutoff, Lemma~\ref{lem:arity-cutoff}).
  The completion closure $\CompCl(\Fft)$ carries a quasi-inverse
  bar-cobar equivalence on the homotopy category
  (Corollary~\ref{cor:completion-closure-equivalence}), stable under
  MC~twisting (Theorem~\ref{thm:mc-twisting-closure}), with completed
  twisting representability
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:completed-twisting-representability}).
  Splits into MC4$^+$ (positive towers) and MC4$^0$ (resonant).
  MC4$^+$ is \textbf{unconditionally solved} by weightwise
  stabilization: for $\mathcal{W}_{1+\infty}$, affine Yangians, and
  positive RTT towers, coefficient stabilization
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:coefficient-stability-criterion}) reduces
  completion to finite truncations.  MC4$^0$ concerns algebras with
  finite resonance rank (Virasoro, non-quadratic
  $\mathcal{W}_N$) and is reduced to a finite-dimensional problem
  by Theorem~\ref{thm:resonance-filtered-bar-cobar}.  The uniform
  PBW bridge (Theorem~\ref{thm:uniform-pbw-bridge}) connects MC1
  to MC4: uniform PBW degeneration plus quotient stabilization
  implies completed bar-cobar duality.
  The \emph{general theorem} (strong completion-tower
  theorem) is proved unconditionally.  What remains is
  \emph{example-specific verification}: for each new
  algebra family beyond the standard landscape, one must
  verify that its coefficient sequences stabilize on finite
  windows and identify the H-level target.  This is a
  finite computation for each family, not a theoretical
  gap.
  \emph{Arithmetic connection}: the spectral curve of the shadow
  Higgs field
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-higgs-field}) has convergence
  radius $|c|/3$ in the arity variable;
  the MC4 completion radius is controlled by the same parameter
  $\lambda_{\mathrm{eff}} = -6/c$
  (Chapter~\ref{chap:arithmetic-shadows},
  Remark~\ref{rem:effective-coupling}).
\item \emph{MC5} (\textbf{analytic part proved}):  Inductive genus
  determination, 2D convergence (no UV renormalization needed),
  analytic-algebraic comparison, and the general HS-sewing criterion
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:general-hs-sewing}: polynomial OPE growth
  plus subexponential sector growth implies convergence at all genera).
  Heisenberg sewing proved (Theorem~\ref{thm:heisenberg-sewing}:
  one-particle Bergman reduction, Fredholm determinant).  The
  genuswise BV/BRST/bar comparison itself remains open; at genus~$0$
  only the algebraic BRST/bar comparison is proved, while the
  moduli-integration/amplitude pairing is conditional.
  Pillar~C (Mok's log-smooth degeneration) provides additional
  inductive structure via rigid special-fibre decomposition.
  \emph{Arithmetic connection}: the sewing--Selberg formula
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:sewing-selberg-formula}) identifies
  $\int_{\cM_{1,1}}\log\det(1{-}K)\cdot E_s\,d\mu
  = -2(2\pi)^{-(s-1)}\Gamma(s{-}1)\zeta(s{-}1)\zeta(s)$;
  the Fredholm determinant of the HS-sewing theorem is the
  same $\det(1{-}K_q)$ whose divisor-sum decomposition
  encodes $\zeta(s)\zeta(s{+}1)$
  (Chapter~\ref{chap:arithmetic-shadows}).
\end{itemize}
\end{remark}

\section{The three concentric rings}
\label{sec:three-rings}
\index{three concentric rings|textbf}
\index{nonlinear characteristic layer|textbf}

The monograph is organized in three concentric rings.

\subsection*{Ring~1: The proved modular Koszul core}
Theorems~A/B/C/D/H, MC1/MC2/MC4, the analytic sewing package of MC5
\textup{(}proved\textup{)},
MC3 (proved for all simple types; Corollary~\ref{cor:mc3-all-types}),
DK-0 through DK-3, and the Koszulness characterization programme
(10 unconditional, 1 conditional, 1 partially proved;
Theorem~\ref{thm:koszul-equivalences-meta}).  This is the spine.  Nothing in the extension
appendices touches it except to cross-reference from it.

\subsection*{Ring~2: The nonlinear characteristic layer}
Before the extension appendices, the modular characteristic was
essentially scalar: the single number~$\kappa(\cA)$ and its
$\lambda_g$ tower, plus the spectral
discriminant~$\Delta_\cA(x)$.  Now there is a hierarchy:
\[
\kappa(\cA)
\;\longrightarrow\;
\Delta_\cA
\;\longrightarrow\;
[\mathfrak{C}_\cA],\;
[\mathfrak{Q}_\cA]
\;\longrightarrow\;
\Lambda_P(\mathfrak{Q}_\cA)
\;\longrightarrow\;
\Theta_\cA.
\]
\begin{itemize}
\item The \emph{nonlinear modular shadows} chapter
  (Chapter~\ref{app:nonlinear-modular-shadows}) makes the
  cubic and quartic jets of the complementarity
  potential~$S_\cA$ into precise, computable invariants with
  clutching laws and a quartic resonance class.
\item The \emph{all-arity master equation} extends the shadow
  tower to arbitrary arity~$r$: the primitive archetypes terminate
  (Gaussian at~$2$, Lie/tree at~$3$, contact at~$4$), while
  Virasoro is the first genuinely infinite tower
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:nms-finite-termination}).
\item The \emph{genus loop operator}~$\Lambda_P$ implements
  non-separating clutching: the genus-$1$ Hessian correction
  $\delta H^{(1)}=\Lambda_P(\mathfrak Q^{(0)})$ is the first
  tensorial modular invariant beyond the $\hat{A}$-genus
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:nms-beyond-ahat}).  For the Virasoro,
  $\delta H^{(1)}_{\mathrm{Vir}}
  =120/[c^2(5c+22)]\cdot x^2$.
\item The \emph{branch-line reductions} appendix
  (Appendix~\ref{app:branch-line-reductions}) extracts exact
  finite-dimensional quotients: the universal genus-$3$
  constant~$7$, genus-$2$ transparency, and the spectral
  cumulant hierarchy.
\item The \emph{ambient complementarity upgrade}
  (\S\ref{sec:ambient-complementarity-lagrangian}) upgrades
  Theorem~C from additive splitting to shifted-symplectic
  Lagrangian geometry: one ambient deformation problem with two
  Lagrangian maps, a complementarity potential~$S_\cA$ whose
  Taylor jets are the nonlinear modular invariants, a derived
  critical locus governing simultaneous self-dual deformations,
  and a fake-complementarity criterion detecting when the dual
  Lagrangian is linear
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:fake-complementarity-criterion}).
\item The \emph{modular bar--Hamiltonian}
  (\S\ref{sec:modular-bar-hamiltonian}) identifies the carrier
  algebra~$\mathfrak{g}^{\mathrm{amb}}_\cA$ with its five-piece
  differential (internal $+$ kernel twist $+$ stable-edge sewing
  $+$ planted-forest correction $+$ genus loop).  The universal
  class~$\Theta_\cA$ is a Maurer--Cartan element in this algebra
  (Definition~\ref{def:modular-bar-hamiltonian}), and the recursive
  extension tower provides the constructive mechanism for building
  it order by order
  (Construction~\ref{constr:obstruction-recursion}).
\item The \emph{modular Chern--Weil transform}
  (\S\ref{sec:modular-chern-weil-transform}) is a single map from
  $\operatorname{MC}(\mathfrak{g}^{\mathrm{amb}}_\cA)$ to the full
  invariant hierarchy: scalar classes, spectral classes, resonance
  classes, and line-kernel data are all projections of
  one Maurer--Cartan element.  The complementarity
  Legendrian~$\Lambda_\cA = j^1\mathfrak{S}_\cA$, the
  complementarity Stokes groupoid, and the phase
  index~$\nu_{\mathrm{nl}}(\cA,u)$ are geometric avatars of the
  same master element.
\item The \emph{quartic resonance class}
  $\mathfrak{R}_{4,g,n}^{\mathrm{mod}}(\cA)$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:nms-clutching-law-modular-resonance}) is the
  first Picard-valued nonlinear characteristic of the theory, with
  clutching law receiving a cubic tree correction
  $\mathfrak{T}_{3,\xi}(\cA)$ on separating boundaries.
\item The \emph{graph-completed Feynman transform package}
  (\S\ref{sec:nms-feynman-transform-programme}) identifies the
  carrier object~$\mathfrak{F}_{\mathrm{mod}}(\cA)$ in which the
  full universal class should live, the full
  \emph{resonance tower}~$\mathfrak{R}^{\mathrm{mod}}_{r}$ for all
  arities~$r \ge 4$, and the \emph{nonlinear
  spectral-branch stack}~$\mathfrak{B}^{\mathrm{nl}}_\cA$.
\item The \emph{shadow archetypes in Part~II}: each standard
  family chapter now computes its nonlinear shadow explicitly.
  Heisenberg is exactly Gaussian
  (\S\ref{sec:heisenberg-shadow-gaussianity}); affine
  $\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_2$ is Lie/tree with critical-level
  emergence (\S\ref{sec:affine-cubic-shadow}); $\beta\gamma$ is
  the contact/quartic primitive with rank-one abelian rigidity
  (\S\ref{sec:betagamma-quartic-birth}); Virasoro and
  $\mathcal{W}_N$ are the first mixed cubic--quartic families with
  infinite shadow towers (\S\ref{sec:mixed-cubic-quartic-shadows}).
  The Virasoro quartic contact coefficient
  $Q^{\mathrm{contact}}_{\mathrm{Vir}} = 10/[c(5c+22)]$;
  genus-$1$ loop ratio
  $\rho^{(1)}_{\mathrm{Vir}} = 240/[c^3(5c+22)]$.
  The \emph{quintic shadow} $S_5^{\mathrm{Vir}}(c) = -48/[c^2(5c+22)]$
  and \emph{sextic shadow} $S_6^{\mathrm{Vir}}(c) = 80(45c+193)/[3c^3(5c+22)^2]$
  are the first explicit arity-$5$ and arity-$6$ computations
  (computed from the convolution recursion $f^2 = Q_L$).
  The sign pattern
  $S_2 > 0$, $S_3 > 0$, $S_4 > 0$, $S_5 < 0$, $S_6 > 0$, $S_7 < 0$
  for $c > 0$ is dictated by the branch-point structure of $\sqrt{Q_L}$.
  For depth-bounded classes: $S_5 = 0$ (classes G, L);
  on the one-dimensional metric, $\beta\gamma$ (class~C) has $S_5 = 1/2 \neq 0$,
  but stratum separation kills the quintic in the full deformation complex.
  The DS depth-increase mechanism at arity~$5$ is verified:
  $\mathfrak{sl}_2$ (depth~$3$, $S_5 = 0$) $\to$
  $\mathrm{Vir}$ (depth~$\infty$, $S_5 \neq 0$) via ghost-sector
  quartic seed; ghost central charge $c_{\mathrm{ghost}} = 2$ (constant).
  The genus-$2$ planted-forest correction
  $\delta_{\mathrm{pf}}^{(2,0)} = S_3(10 S_3 - \kappa)/48$;
  for Virasoro $\delta_{\mathrm{pf}}^{(2,0)} = -(c-40)/48$.
\item The \emph{envelope-shadow functor}
  (\S\ref{sec:concordance-nishinaka-vicedo}) upgrades the shadow
  tower from a case-by-case invariant to a functor on Lie conformal
  input $R \mapsto \Thetaenv(R) := \Theta(\Uvert(R))$, using the
  Nishinaka--Vicedo factorization-envelope pipeline.  The
  envelope-shadow complexity $\chienv(R)$ recovers the
  G/L/C/M classification; the arity-$r$ shadow depends only on
  the $(r{+}1)$-jet (Proposition~\ref{prop:finite-jet-rigidity})
  and is polynomial of degree~$\leq r{-}1$ in the
  central-extension parameter
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:polynomial-level-dependence}).
\item The \emph{universal Maurer--Cartan principle}
  (\S\ref{sec:nms-universal-mc-principle}) establishes the modular
  convolution algebra~$\mathfrak{g}_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}}$ as a modular
  $L_\infty$ algebra (with the dg~Lie algebra as its strict model), and the shadow tower
  $\kappa \to \Delta \to \mathfrak{C} \to \mathfrak{Q} \to \Theta$
  arising as evaluation of the universal MC element~$\Theta_\cA$
  on specific moduli cycles.  The five-component differential
  $D = d_{A_\infty} + d_{\mathrm{sew}} + \hbar\Delta + d_r$
  is automatic from the single MC equation.  The dg~Lie model
  is the strict shadow of the $L_\infty$ structure; bar-cobar
  preserves quasi-isos because it is a quantum $L_\infty$ functor.
\item The \emph{non-renormalization theorem}
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:non-renormalization-tree}, ProvedElsewhere,
  Dimofte--Niu--Py) validates all tree-level computations: for
  quasi-linear theories (all HT-twisted 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$), the
  $A_\infty$ operations and the $r$-matrix are exact at tree level.
  Loop corrections enter only through the genus-raising BV
  operator~$\Delta$.
\item The \emph{polarized scattering package}
  (\S\ref{sec:nms-polarized-scattering-programme}) replaces the
  one-colour Maurer--Cartan problem by a bipartite machine:
  a polarized modular graph
  algebra~$\mathcal{G}^{\pm}_{\mathrm{mod}}(\cA)$ with
  same-colour vanishing, a \emph{resonance scattering
  diagram}~$\mathfrak{Scat}(\cA)$, a categorified
  \emph{complementarity schober}~$\mathfrak{Sch}(\cA)$, and a
  \emph{modular wavefunction}~$\Psi_\cA$ satisfying the quantum
  master equation.  Four conjectural theorems (bipartite
  vanishing, quartic lift, resonance wall-crossing, quantization)
  organize the forward attack.
\item The \emph{multi-variable shadow tower}
  (\S\ref{sec:nms-multivariable-shadow}) extends the shadow
  construction to algebras with multiple strong generators
  (e.g., $\mathcal{W}_3$ with generators $T,W$).  The
  \emph{Kac-shadow singularity principle}
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:kac-shadow-singularity}) identifies
  denominators of shadow coefficients with Kac determinant
  factors.  The \emph{shadow subalgebra autonomy theorem}
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-subalgebra-autonomy}) states that
  the shadow tower of~$\cA$ restricts to the shadow tower of
  any strongly generated subalgebra, and the
  \emph{$\mathcal{W}$-line alternating vanishing}
  (Corollary~\ref{cor:w-line-alternating-vanishing}) forces
  $\mathrm{Sh}_{2r+1}^{W\text{-pure}} = 0$ for all~$r$.
  Drinfeld--Sokolov reduction strictly increases shadow depth
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:ds-shadow-depth-increase}):
  $r_{\max}(\mathcal{W}_N) \geq r_{\max}(V_k(\fg)) + 1$.
\item The \emph{Kac--Chevalley factorization question},
  whether the Kac determinant and the Chevalley discriminant
  factor through a common polynomial, is \textbf{resolved as
  spurious}: the two objects are algebraically independent.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{Ring~3: The physics-facing extension problems}
Three axes, each with its own appendix chain:
\begin{enumerate}
\item \emph{The $\mathcal{W}$-algebra axis.}
  Completed Koszulity is ubiquitous (every affine
  $\mathcal{W}$-algebra at generic level); strict Koszulity is
  exceptional.  The subregular family
  $\mathcal{W}_n^{(2)}$ exhibits unbounded canonical homotopy
  arity.
\item \emph{The Yangian/RTT axis and the Bridge Theorem.}
  Three layers: local RTT kernel, completed envelope, boundary
  quotient.  The shift belongs to the boundary quotient, not
  the local kernel.  The rank-one test case produces the
  quantized Kleinian surface.
  The \emph{Bridge Theorem project}
  (Remark~\ref{rem:bridge-theorem-programme};
  Theorem~\ref{thm:bridge-criterion})
  is now the central remaining target: the full triple
  equivalence
  $\mathrm{Fact}^{\Eone}_{\mathrm{ord}} \simeq
  \mathrm{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_\cA) \simeq
  \mathrm{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_\cA))^{\mathrm{op}}$
  decomposes into four sub-targets~B1--B4 with a proved criterion
  theorem (B1$+$B2$+$B4 $\Rightarrow$ full bridge).
\item \emph{The holographic/celestial axis.}
  Protected transform calculus (dual transform, transposition,
  Weyl sewing, metaplectic anomaly) built directly from the
  proved core.
  Volume~II develops the bulk--boundary--line Koszul triangle
  $A_{\mathrm{bulk}} \simeq Z_{\mathrm{der}}(\text{boundary})
  \simeq \mathrm{HH}^\bullet(\cA^!)$.
  The \emph{holographic modular Koszul datum}
  $\mathcal{H}(T) = (\cA, \cA^!, \mathcal{C}, r(z), \Theta_\cA,
  \nabla^{\mathrm{hol}})$
  (Definition~\ref{def:holographic-modular-koszul-datum})
  packages the full HT holographic system into a single modular
  MC problem: the dg-shifted Yangian $r(z)$ is the binary
  genus-zero collision residue of~$\Theta_\cA$, and the 2026
  exact sphere-correlator matching~\cite{GZ26} is the genus-zero
  matrix-element shadow of this datum.  Five theorem targets
  decompose the programme: boundary--defect realization
  (Conjecture~\ref{conj:boundary-defect-realization}),
  Yangian-shadow
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:yangian-shadow-theorem}; \textbf{proved}),
  sphere reconstruction
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:sphere-reconstruction}; \textbf{proved}),
  quartic resonance obstruction
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:quartic-resonance-obstruction}; \textbf{proved}),
  and singular-fiber descent
  (Conjecture~\ref{conj:singular-fiber-descent}).
  The factorisation quantum-group envelope~\cite{Latyntsev23}
  supplies the categorical home beyond the meromorphic line category,
  and the HT deformation-quantization functor
  (Conjecture~\ref{conj:ht-deformation-quantization})
  bridges classical PVA data to the quantum modular Koszul package.
  The landscape of worked physics examples now includes:
  free chiral vortex lines with explicit $r$-matrix
  (\S\ref{sec:betagamma-vortex-lines}),
  affine PVA $\to$ Chern--Simons action
  (\S\ref{sec:affine-ht-chern-simons}),
  SQED--XYZ mirror symmetry as bar-cobar equivalence,
  non-renormalization of tree-level operations
  (\S\ref{sec:non-renormalization-tree}),
  superpotential $A_\infty$ truncation
  (\S\ref{sec:superpotential-ainfty-truncation}),
  Virasoro phase space as Teichm\"uller geometry
  (\S\ref{subsec:virasoro-teichmuller-phase-space}),
  level-rank duality as Koszul duality,
  monopole operators via affine Grassmannian modifications,
  Costello's M2-brane double-loop model
  (\S\ref{sec:m2-brane-double-loop}),
  SuperVirasoro $\to$ 3d supergravity,
  SQCD boundary algebra,
  Witten diagrams in twisted holography,
  $N=4$ global symmetry matching,
  the deformed conifold,
  and $\mathcal{W}_N \to$ higher-spin gauge theory.
\end{enumerate}

\subsection*{The unifying principle}
The organizing principle of all three rings:
\emph{one object, one equation, and a proof obligation
at each level.}
The modular $L_\infty$ convolution
algebra~$\mathfrak{g}_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}}$ is the ambient
home.  An algebra structure on~$\cA$ IS a Maurer--Cartan
element~$\Theta_\cA \in
\mathrm{MC}(\mathfrak{g}_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}})$.
The shadow tower, the genus tower, the graph sums, and
the shadow archetypes are \emph{natural consequences} of
this framework.  However, each level of the tower
(Ring~1: the proved core; Ring~2: the finite-order shadow
engine; Ring~3: the physics-facing frontier) requires
independent verification that the MC equation's
projections produce the claimed invariants.  Ring~1 is
fully proved.  Ring~2 is proved at finite order.  Ring~3
contains significant open problems (non-principal W-duality, analytic completion).
The dg~Lie model is the strict computational avatar;
the $L_\infty$ structure is the reason bar-cobar is a
Quillen equivalence.
Filtration controls the extension tower:
In Ring~2, the complementarity potential has a Taylor filtration
whose jets are the nonlinear shadows.  In Ring~3, the MC4 splitting
(Remark~\ref{rem:mc4-positive-vs-resonant}) separates
the completion problem:
positive towers ($\mathcal{W}_{1+\infty}$, Yangians) are
solved by weight stabilization
(Theorem~\ref{thm:stabilized-completion-positive});
resonant towers (Virasoro, non-quadratic $\mathcal{W}_N$) require the
resonance-filtered construction
(Theorem~\ref{thm:resonance-filtered-bar-cobar}),
with the same-family shadow $\mathrm{Vir}_{26-c}$ reinterpreted as
the depth-zero resonance shadow
(Remark~\ref{rem:virasoro-resonance-model}).
In Ring~3 (holography),
the composite filtration separates the wedge from the nonlinear
obstruction tower.

The five main theorems establish \emph{existence of duality}.
The three rings develop the \emph{structure of the invariants
that duality produces}.

\begin{proposition}[Five main theorems as MC projections]
\label{prop:five-theorems-mc-projections}
\label{rem:top-down-architecture}% backward compatibility
\ClaimStatusProvedHere
\index{top-down architecture|textbf}
\index{five main theorems!as MC projections}
Theorems~A--D and~H are projections of the master MC element $\Theta_\cA \in \mathrm{MC}(\gAmod)$:
\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{cll}
\toprule
Projection & Theorem & Content \\
\midrule
$\alpha_{\Theta}$ (twisting morphism) & A & $B_\kappa \dashv \Omega_\kappa$ \\
$D_\cA^2 = 0$ (bar-intrinsic) & B & $\Omega(B(\cA)) \xrightarrow{\sim} \cA$ \\
$\mathrm{tr}\,\pi_{2,\bullet}(\Theta_\cA)$ & C & $Q_g(\cA) + Q_g(\cA^!) = H^*(\overline{\mathcal{M}}_g, Z(\cA))$ \\
$\pi_{\mathrm{sc}}(\Theta_\cA)$ & D & $\kappa(\cA)$ universal, $\hat{A}$-genus GF \\
$\pi_{\mathrm{HH}}(\Theta_\cA)$ & H & $\mathrm{ChirHoch}^*(\cA)$ polynomial \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}
The shadow Postnikov tower
$\Theta_\cA^{\leq r}$ consists of finite-order truncations; the
obstruction classes~$o_{r+1}(\cA)$ classify shadow depth into the
four archetypes
$\mathsf{G}$/$\mathsf{L}$/$\mathsf{C}$/$\mathsf{M}$
(Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-archetype-classification}).
The full MC element
$\Theta_\cA = \varprojlim \Theta_\cA^{\leq r}$ is proved by the
bar-intrinsic construction
(Theorem~\ref{thm:mc2-bar-intrinsic}).
\end{proposition}


%% ====================================================================
%%  INTRINSIC KOSZULNESS: THE CHARACTERIZATION PROGRAMME
%% ====================================================================
\section{Intrinsic Koszulness: the characterization programme}
\label{sec:concordance-koszulness-programme}
\index{Koszul property!characterization programme|textbf}
\index{chiral Koszulness!intrinsic characterization|textbf}

The PBW criterion (Theorem~\ref{thm:pbw-koszulness-criterion})
detects chiral Koszulness for every standard family but does
not characterize it intrinsically.  This section is the
constitutional index for the intrinsic characterization
programme.  Full statements and proofs live in the source
chapters cited below.

%% ------------------------------------------------------------------
\subsection{The meta-theorem: twelve characterizations}
\label{subsec:concordance-koszulness-meta-theorem}
\index{Koszul property!equivalences|textbf}

Let $\cA$ be an augmented chiral algebra with PBW
filtration~$F_\bullet$.  The full meta-theorem is
Theorem~\ref{thm:koszul-equivalences-meta} in
Chapter~\ref{chap:koszul-pairs}.
Items are listed in the meta-theorem's numbering, so that
\textup{(\ref{item:kp-def})}--\textup{(\ref{item:kp-dmod})}
in the concordance and in the chapter are identical.

\medskip\noindent
\textbf{Unconditional equivalences} (i)--(x):

\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)},ref=\roman*]
\item\label{item:kp-def}
  Chirally Koszul (Definition~\ref{def:chiral-koszul-morphism}).
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-pbw}
  PBW spectral sequence on $\barBgeom(\cA)$ collapses at~$E_2$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:pbw-koszulness-criterion}).
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-ainfty}
  Minimal $A_\infty$-model has $m_n = 0$ for $n \ge 3$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:ainfty-koszul-characterization}).
  Converse via Keller classicality.
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-ext}
  Ext diagonal: $\operatorname{Ext}^{p,q}_\cA(\omega_X,\omega_X)=0$ for $p \neq q$
  (Theorem~\ref{conj:ext-diagonal-vanishing}).
  Off-diagonal $d_r$ contradicts concentration.
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-barcobar}
  Bar-cobar counit $\Omegach(\barBch(\cA)) \to \cA$ is a quasi-isomorphism
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:bar-cobar-inversion-qi}).
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-barrbeck}
  Barr--Beck--Lurie comparison for $\barBch \dashv \Omegach$ is an equivalence
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:barr-beck-lurie-koszulness}).
  Conservativity + totalization on log-FM strata.
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-facthom}
  Factorization homology $\textstyle\int_X \cA$ in degree~$0$ for all smooth~$X$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:fh-concentration-koszulness}).
  Bar = FH; genus-$0$ concentration forces $E_2$-collapse.
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-hochschild}
  $\ChirHoch^*(\cA)$ polynomial, vanishing outside $\{0,1,2\}$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:main-koszul-hoch}).
  For single-generator algebras with no simple pole in the OPE,
  $\ChirHoch^1 = \mathbb{C}$ (outer derivation survives because
  the zero mode is central); for algebras with simple poles,
  $\ChirHoch^1 = 0$ (all derivations inner).
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-nullvec}
  Kac--Shapovalov: $\det G_h \neq 0$ in the bar-relevant range
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:kac-shapovalov-koszulness}).
  Non-degeneracy forces PBW injectivity; $d_r$-exactness contradicts pairing.
  \hfill \checkmark
\item\label{item:kp-fmbdy}
  FM boundary acyclicity: $H^k(i_S^!\,\barBgeom_n(\cA)) = 0$ for $k \neq 0$, all strata~$S$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:fm-boundary-acyclicity}).
  Stratum-by-stratum PBW; binary collision forces injectivity.
  \hfill \checkmark
\end{enumerate}

\medskip\noindent
\textbf{Conditional/partial in general; (xi) unconditional for standard landscape} (xi)--(xii):

\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)},ref=\roman*,resume]
\item\label{item:kp-lagrangian}
  Lagrangian complementarity: $\mathcal{M}_\cA, \mathcal{M}_{\cA^!} \hookrightarrow \mathcal{M}_{\mathrm{comp}}$ are $(-1)$-shifted Lagrangian
  (Theorem~\ref{conj:lagrangian-koszulness}).
  PTVV derived intersection.  Perfectness verified for the standard
  landscape (Proposition~\ref{prop:lagrangian-perfectness},
  Corollary~\ref{cor:lagrangian-unconditional}): unconditional at
  non-critical, non-degenerate levels.
  \hfill \checkmark\;(\emph{unconditional for standard landscape})
\item\label{item:kp-dmod}
  $\mathcal{D}$-module purity: $\barBgeom_n(\cA)$ pure, $\operatorname{Ch}(\barBgeom_n) \subset \bigcup_S T^*_S\overline{C}_n(X)$.
  Implied by FM boundary acyclicity~(\ref{item:kp-fmbdy}).
  \hfill (\emph{one-directional}; $(\ref{item:kp-fmbdy})\Rightarrow(\ref{item:kp-dmod})$ proved, converse open)
\end{enumerate}

%% ------------------------------------------------------------------
\subsection{Sufficient conditions for chiral Koszulness}
\label{subsec:concordance-koszulness-sufficient}
\index{Koszul property!sufficient conditions|textbf}

Two sufficient conditions for chiral Koszulness are established:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\alph*)}]
\item \emph{PBW universality}
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:pbw-universality}):
  freely strongly generated vertex algebras are chirally Koszul.
  Applies to: $V_k(\fg)$ (all $k$), $\mathrm{Vir}_c$ (all $c$),
  $\mathcal{W}^k(\fg)$ (Miura free generators).
\item \emph{Kac--Shapovalov criterion}
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:kac-shapovalov-koszulness}):
  $\det G_h \neq 0$ in the bar-relevant range.
  Applies to: $V_k(\fg)$, $\mathrm{Vir}_c$ at generic $c$.
\end{enumerate}

Rationality, $C_2$-cofiniteness, and semisimple Zhu algebra remain
important \emph{finiteness} inputs for simple quotients at
non-degenerate admissible levels, but they do not by themselves
identify the Ext groups computed by the bar complex with Ext in the
ordinary semisimple module category.  Accordingly no unconditional
rationality criterion for chiral Koszulness is claimed in the
constitution.

%% ------------------------------------------------------------------
\subsection{Operadic complexity}
\label{subsec:concordance-operadic-complexity}
\index{operadic complexity|textbf}
\index{shadow Postnikov tower!operadic complexity}

\begin{theorem}[Operadic complexity;
  \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{thm:operadic-complexity-concordance}%
\index{operadic complexity|textbf}
For a chiral Koszul algebra~$\cA$, the three invariants
coincide: $r_{\max}(\cA) = d_\infty(\cA) = f_\infty(\cA)$,
where $r_{\max}$ is the shadow depth
(Theorem~\ref{thm:nms-finite-termination}), $d_\infty$ is
the $A_\infty$-depth (largest $n$ with $m_n^{\mathrm{tr}}
\neq 0$), and $f_\infty$ is the $L_\infty$-formality level
(largest $n$ with $\ell_n^{(0),\mathrm{tr}} \neq 0$ on
$\mathfrak{g}_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}}$).
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
The equality $r_{\max} = f_\infty$ is
Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-formality-identification}:
the arity-$r$ shadow $\operatorname{Sh}_r(\cA)$ equals
$\ell_r^{(0),\mathrm{tr}}$ evaluated on the truncated
MC element at every arity, so $\operatorname{Sh}_r = 0$
iff $\ell_r^{(0),\mathrm{tr}} = 0$ on $H^*$.

For $f_\infty = d_\infty$: the cyclic deformation complex
$\Defcyc(\cA)$ carries both an $A_\infty$ structure
(from the bar differential) and an $L_\infty$ structure
(from the convolution bracket).  On the genus-$0$ part,
the Lie bracket $[-,-]^{(0)}$ is the antisymmetrization
of the associative composition, so the transferred
brackets satisfy
$\ell_r^{(0),\mathrm{tr}} =
\operatorname{Alt}(m_r^{\mathrm{tr}})$.
The HPL tree formula~\eqref{eq:tree-formula-general}
is universal in~$r$: the same set $\mathsf{Trees}_r$
of planar rooted trees with $r$ leaves, the same
homotopy~$h$ on internal edges, and the same vertex
evaluations appear in both the $A_\infty$ and
$L_\infty$ transfers.  Since antisymmetrization is
injective on the cyclic deformation complex
(the cyclic symmetry ensures no cancellation between
distinct tree contributions), $m_r^{\mathrm{tr}} = 0$
iff $\ell_r^{(0),\mathrm{tr}} = 0$.  Hence
$d_\infty = f_\infty$.
\end{proof}

\noindent
The shadow--formality dictionary and archetype verification:

\begin{center}
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.15}
\begin{tabular}{@{}llll@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Shadow} & \textbf{$L_\infty$ bracket}
  & \textbf{Family} & $r_{\max}$ \\
\midrule
$\kappa$ (arity~$2$) & $\ell_2$
  & Heisenberg & $2$ \\
$\mathfrak{C}$ (arity~$3$) & $\ell_3^{\mathrm{tr}}$
  & Affine $\widehat{\fg}_k$ & $3$ \\
$\mathfrak{Q}$ (arity~$4$) & $\ell_4^{\mathrm{tr}}$
  & $\beta\gamma$ & $4$ \\
full tower & all $\ell_k^{\mathrm{tr}}$
  & $\mathrm{Vir}_c$ & $\infty$ \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}


%% ------------------------------------------------------------------
\subsection{Shadow depth classification}
\label{subsec:concordance-shadow-depth-classes}
\index{shadow depth!classification}
\index{Koszul property!shadow depth classes}

Shadow depth is orthogonal to Koszulness: all standard
families are chirally Koszul, yet their shadow depths differ.
See Theorem~\ref{thm:nms-archetype-trichotomy}.

\begin{center}
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.15}
\begin{tabular}{@{}clll@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Class} & \textbf{Name} & \textbf{Criterion}
  & \textbf{Examples} \\
\midrule
\textbf{G} & Gaussian
  & $r_{\max}=2$; formal
  & $\mathcal{H}_k$, free fermion, rank-$1$ lattice \\
\textbf{L} & Lie
  & $r_{\max}=3$; $\mathfrak{C}\neq 0$, $o_4=0$ (Jacobi)
  & $V_k(\fg)$ \\
\textbf{C} & Contact
  & $r_{\max}=4$; $\mathfrak{Q}\neq 0$, $o_5=0$ (abelian rigidity)
  & $\beta\gamma$, symplectic fermion\,? \\
\textbf{M} & Mixed
  & $r_{\max}=\infty$; non-formal
  & $\mathrm{Vir}_c$, $\mathcal{W}_N$, $Y(\fg)$ ($\Eone$-shadow depth from RTT tower) \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\noindent
The inclusions $\mathbf{G} \subset \mathbf{L} \subset
\mathbf{C} \subset \mathbf{M}$ are proper.  Shadow depth
classifies the complexity of~$\Theta_\cA$, not whether the
bar complex is acyclic
(Remark~\ref{rem:koszulness-vs-shadow-depth}).

\medskip\noindent\textbf{Fine classification and arithmetic content.}
The coarse $\mathbf{G}/\mathbf{L}/\mathbf{C}/\mathbf{M}$
partition admits a finer grading by the exact depth
$d\in\{2,3,4,5,\ldots\}\cup\{\infty\}$; every finite value
is realized by even unimodular lattice VOAs of increasing rank
(Chapter~\ref{chap:arithmetic-shadows},
\S\ref{sec:higher-depths}).  The shadow--spectral correspondence
(Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-spectral-correspondence}) identifies
$d-1$ with the number of critical lines of the constrained
Epstein zeta $\varepsilon^c_s(\cA)$, whose $L$-function
factorization reflects the modular-form decomposition of the
theta function.  The first five lattice examples are:

\begin{center}
\small
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.1}
\begin{tabular}{@{}lccl@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Algebra} & \textbf{Depth} & \textbf{Lines}
  & \textbf{$L$-function content} \\
\midrule
$V_{\bZ}$ & $2$ & $1$ & $\zeta(2s)$ \\
$V_{\bZ^2}$, $V_{A_2}$ & $2$ & $1$
  & $\zeta_{\bQ(\sqrt{-d})}(s)$ \\
$V_{E_8}$ & $3$ & $2$
  & $\zeta(s)\cdot\zeta(s{-}3)$ \\
$V_{\mathrm{Leech}}$ & $4$ & $3$
  & $\zeta(s)\cdot\zeta(s{-}11)\cdot L(s,\Delta_{12})$ \\
Rank-$48$ lattice & $5$ & $4$
  & $+$ second cusp form \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\noindent
The sewing--Selberg formula
(Theorem~\ref{thm:sewing-selberg-formula}):
$\int_{\cM_{1,1}}\log\det(1{-}K)\cdot E_s\,d\mu
=-2(2\pi)^{-(s-1)}\Gamma(s{-}1)\,\zeta(s{-}1)\zeta(s)$.

\smallskip\noindent
The depth decomposition
(Theorem~\ref{thm:depth-decomposition}):
$d(\cA) = 1 + d_{\mathrm{arith}} + d_{\mathrm{alg}}$,
where $d_{\mathrm{arith}}$ counts holomorphic Hecke eigenforms
(determines critical lines) and $d_{\mathrm{alg}}$ measures
non-holomorphic OPE complexity (invisible to $L$-functions).
For lattice VOAs: $d_{\mathrm{alg}} = 0$; for Virasoro
minimal models: $d_{\mathrm{arith}}$ finite,
$d_{\mathrm{alg}} = \infty$.  The Borel sum of the
Virasoro shadow series gives $-\log(1 + 6t/c)$ at leading
order (Proposition~\ref{prop:shadow-gf-borel}).

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Shadow growth rate}
(Definition~\ref{def:shadow-growth-rate},
Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-radius}).
For class~$\mathbf{M}$ algebras, the shadow growth rate
$\rho(\cA) = \sqrt{9\alpha^2 + 2\Delta}\,/\,(2|\kappa|)$
refines shadow depth into a \emph{continuous invariant}:
the exponential growth rate of the shadow tower coefficients.
The shadow generating function
$H(t) = t^2\sqrt{Q_L(t)}$ has convergence
radius $R = 1/\rho$, and the asymptotic transfer theorem
gives $S_r \sim A\,\rho^r \cdot r^{-5/2}\cos(r\theta + \varphi)$.
For $\mathrm{Vir}_c$:
$\rho(c) = \sqrt{(180c{+}872)/((5c{+}22)c^2)}$.
The critical cubic $5c^3 + 22c^2 - 180c - 872 = 0$ has unique
positive real root $c_\star \approx 6.125$; for
$c > c_\star$ the tower converges ($\rho < 1$), for
$c < c_\star$ it diverges.  Koszul duality
$c \mapsto 26 - c$ acts on~$\rho$; at $c = 13$
the shadow growth rate is self-dual ($\rho \approx 0.467$).
The branch-point argument
$\arg(t_0)/\pi$ increases monotonically toward~$1$ as
$c \to \infty$, encoding the near-alternation of signs.
The convergent regime $c > c_\star$ connects to the
arithmetic programme: $\rho$ controls the abscissa of
convergence of the shadow--Epstein zeta
$\varepsilon^c_s(\cA)$.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{General Vieta structure}
(Theorem~\ref{thm:vieta-shadow-growth}).
The shadow growth rate $\rho_L = \sqrt{q_2/q_0}$ is the
ratio of the quadratic to constant coefficient of~$Q_L$,
a consequence of Vieta's theorem for the
branch-point product.
The critical surface $\{q_0 = q_2\}$ in the shadow metric
moduli space $\mathcal{M}_{\mathrm{sm}}$ is
characterized geometrically:
\emph{the branch points of~$Q_L$ lie on the unit circle}.
No family-specific data enters.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Multi-line structure and Virasoro bottleneck}
(Definition~\ref{def:multi-line-shadow-radius},
Proposition~\ref{prop:virasoro-bottleneck}).
For algebras with multiple primary lines,
$\rho(\cA) = \sup_L \rho_L$.
The Virasoro subsector (T-line) controls the
algebra-level growth rate: every $\cW_N$ algebra has
$\rho(\cW_N) = \rho_T = \rho(\mathrm{Vir}_c)$.
Higher-spin lines have smaller~$\rho$ due to stronger
Kac-denominator suppression of the quartic seed.
Example: $\cW_3$ has $c_T^\star \approx 6.125$
(T-line) but $c_W^\star \approx 1.187$ (W-line),
with $\rho_W^2 = 30720/(c^2(5c{+}22)^3)$.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Koszul exchange of regimes}
(Theorem~\ref{thm:koszul-exchange-regimes}).
For one-parameter families with conductor~$K$ and
Verdier involution $c \mapsto K - c$:
three regimes (I: $\cA$ divergent/$\cA^!$ convergent;
II: both convergent; III: reverse of I).
The convergence window $(c_\star, K - c_\star)$
has fraction $(K - 2c_\star)/K \to 1$ as $K \to \infty$
(Proposition~\ref{prop:propagator-universality}):
$\rho_T(K_N/2) \sim 12/K_N \to 0$.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{DS depth increase.}
Under Drinfeld--Sokolov reduction
$V_k(\slN) \to \mathcal{W}_k(\slN)$, the shadow growth
rate jumps from $\rho = 0$ (class~$\mathbf{L}$, depth~$3$)
to $\rho > 0$ (class~$\mathbf{M}$, depth~$\infty$).
The ghost sector creates all quartic and higher shadows
via BRST cohomology: the DS reduction does not preserve~$\rho$,
but the $\mathcal{W}_N$ T-line shadow radius equals the
Virasoro shadow radius at the DS central charge
$c_{\mathcal{W}_N}(k)$, consistent with the conjectural
$\Theta_{\mathcal{W}_N} = H^0_{Q_{\mathrm{DS}}}(\Theta_{V_k
\otimes \mathcal{F}_{\mathrm{gh}}})$.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Arithmetic threshold}
(Remark~\ref{rem:arithmetic-threshold}).
$\rho < 1$: shadow--Epstein zeta entire.
$\rho = 1$: convergent for $\operatorname{Re}(s) > -3/2$.
$\rho > 1$: divergent, Borel-regularized.
The critical $c_\star$ is the threshold between
direct and regularized spectral decomposition.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Hamilton--Jacobi master equation}
(Theorem~\ref{thm:hamilton-jacobi-shadow}).
On an $N$-dimensional primary deformation space, the nonlinear
shadow generating function
$U(x) = \sum_{r \geq 3} \mathrm{Sh}_r(x_1, \dotsc, x_N)$
satisfies the Hamilton--Jacobi equation
$2\,E(U) + \frac{1}{2}\|\nabla U\|_H^2 = R(x)$,
where $E$ is the Euler operator,
$\|\nabla f\|_H^2 = \sum_i P_i\,(\partial_i f)^2$
is the $H$-norm with propagators $P_i = 1/\kappa_i$,
and the source $R$ is determined entirely by arities~$3$
and~$4$.  On each autonomous primary line, the
Hamilton--Jacobi equation reduces to the Riccati equation of
Theorem~\ref{thm:riccati-algebraicity}.  Verified
computationally for~$\cW_3$ through arity~$7$.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Shadow finite determination}
(Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-finite-determination}).
The full infinite shadow Postnikov tower is uniquely
determined by finite data at arities~$2$, $3$, $4$:
the curvatures $\kappa_1, \dotsc, \kappa_N$, the cubic shadow
$\mathrm{Sh}_3 \in \mathrm{Sym}^3(V^*)$, and the quartic shadow
$\mathrm{Sh}_4 \in \mathrm{Sym}^4(V^*)$.
The Hamilton--Jacobi recursion determines
$\mathrm{Sh}_r$ for all $r \geq 5$ with rational-function
coefficients in the seed data.  For~$\cW_3$ with
$\mathbb{Z}_2$ parity: exactly~$7$ parameters
($\kappa_T$, $\kappa_W$, $\alpha_T$, $\beta_{TW}$,
$Q_{TT}$, $Q_{TW}$, $Q_{WW}$) determine the full
$2$D tower at all arities
(Corollary~\ref{cor:w3-reconstruction}).

%% ------------------------------------------------------------------
\subsection{Geometric, physics, and categorical
  characterizations}
\label{subsec:concordance-further-characterizations}
\index{Koszul property!geometric characterizations}
\index{Koszul property!physics characterizations}
\index{Koszul property!categorical characterizations}

\noindent\textbf{Geometric.}
\begin{itemize}[nosep]
\item \emph{Ran-space formality}: $E_2$-collapse $\Leftrightarrow$ genuswise bar-cobar formality $\Leftrightarrow$ $\tilde{m}_n^{(g)} = 0$ for $n \ge 3$ (Proposition~\ref{prop:e2-collapse-formality}); coherent extension to all $\operatorname{Ran}^{\le n}$ is open.
\item \emph{Tropical Koszulness}: acyclicity of $\barBgeom^{\mathrm{trop}}(\cA)$ for the planted-forest differential (Definition~\ref{def:planted-forest-coefficient-algebra}, Theorem~\ref{thm:planted-forest-tropicalization}).
\item \emph{Curve independence}: chiral Koszulness depends on formal-disk data, not on~$X$; higher-genus propagation governed by MK1--MK3 (Theorem~\ref{thm:genus-graded-koszul}) and the exceptional set~$\Sigma(\fg)$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:bar-cohomology-level-independence}).
\end{itemize}

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Physics.}
\begin{itemize}[nosep]
\item \emph{One-loop exactness}: PBW $E_2$-collapse IS one-loop exactness (Remark~\ref{rem:koszulness-vs-shadow-depth}).
\item \emph{Kac--Shapovalov}: $\det G_h \neq 0$ in bar-relevant range $\Leftrightarrow$ Koszul (Theorem~\ref{thm:kac-shapovalov-koszulness}); proved for $V_k(\fg)$ (Proposition~\ref{prop:pbw-universality}).  For simple admissible quotients $L_k(\fg)$ this route is blocked by null vectors in the bar-relevant range.
\item \emph{Rationality / semisimplicity}: strong finiteness input for non-degenerate admissible levels, but not an unconditional Koszul criterion.  Ordinary semisimplicity controls Zhu theory and character formulas; the comparison with the bar-complex Ext groups remains part of the live admissible-level audit.
\item \emph{$C_2$-cofiniteness}: orthogonal to Koszulness; Koszul duality maps $C_2$-cofinite to non-$C_2$-cofinite.
\item \emph{Critical level}: $V_{-h^\vee}(\fg)$ is uncurved ($\kappa=0$), self-dual, center~$= \mathfrak{z}(\widehat{\fg})$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:critical-level-cohomology}).
\end{itemize}

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Categorical.}
\begin{itemize}[nosep]
\item \emph{$t$-exactness}: $\barBch \colon \operatorname{FactMod}(\cA) \to \operatorname{FactCoMod}(\cA^!)$ exact for PBW/$\Omega$ $t$-structures (Proposition~\ref{prop:koszul-t-structures}).
\item \emph{Barr--Beck--Lurie}: effective descent for bar-cobar (Remark~\ref{rem:construction-vs-resolution}).
\item \emph{Semi-orthogonal decomposition}: weight-indexed SOD on $\operatorname{FactMod}(\cA)$ is split iff Koszul.
\item \emph{BGG}: bar resolution of $V_k(\fg)$-modules is linear; Koszul involution maps BGG to Cousin on $\operatorname{Gr}_G$ (Corollary~\ref{cor:bgg-koszul-involution}).
\item \emph{Convolution formality}: $\mathfrak{g}_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}}$ formal iff one-channel; stronger than Koszulness.
\item \emph{MC smoothness}: $\operatorname{MC}(\mathfrak{g}_\cA^{\mathrm{mod}})$ smooth at~$\Theta_\cA$ iff Koszul.
\end{itemize}


%% ------------------------------------------------------------------
\subsection{Bifunctor obstruction}
\label{subsec:concordance-bifunctor-obstruction}
\index{Robert-Nicoud--Wierstra!bifunctor obstruction}
\index{Koszul property!bifunctor obstruction}

The RNW no-bifunctor obstruction \cite{RNW19}
(\S\ref{sec:concordance-three-pillars}, identification
theorem~7) is structural: $\operatorname{hom}_\alpha(
\mathcal{C},\mathcal{A})$ extends to $\infty$-morphisms in
either slot separately but not both.  Koszulness does not kill
it; Koszulness makes it irrelevant by factoring all
constructions one slot at a time
(Theorem~\ref{thm:quillen-equivalence-chiral}).  This is why
the MC3 strategy
(Theorem~\ref{thm:mc3-type-a-resolution}) succeeds.
\label{rem:concordance-bifunctor-koszul}


%% ------------------------------------------------------------------
\subsection{Computational diagnostics}
\label{subsec:concordance-computational-diagnostics}
\index{Koszul property!computational diagnostics}
\index{bar generating function!algebraicity}

The bar generating function $\overline{P}_\cA(x,t)$ is
algebraic of degree~$2$ in~$t$ for all standard families with
$\dim\fg \le 8$, sharing the discriminant
$\Delta_\cA(x) = (1{-}3x)(1{+}x)$
across $\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_2$, $\beta\gamma$, and
Virasoro (Theorem~\ref{thm:ds-bar-gf-discriminant}).

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Decision tree.}\enspace
(1) Pole order ($1 \Rightarrow$ G; $2 \Rightarrow$ L+).
(2) Freely generated $\Rightarrow$ Koszul (Proposition~\ref{prop:pbw-universality}).
(3) PBW + classical Koszulness of $\operatorname{gr}_F\cA$ (Theorem~\ref{thm:pbw-koszulness-criterion}).
(4) Bar Betti diagonal concentration (Corollary~\ref{cor:bar-cohomology-koszul-dual}).
(5) Generating function fit $\to$ discriminant.

\smallskip\noindent\textbf{Priority computations.}
\begin{itemize}[nosep]
\item $\mathcal{W}_4$ bar Betti numbers (Class~M + discriminant universality).
\item Bigraded Virasoro to $(n,h)=(4,16)$ (quartic resonance at GF level).
\item Symplectic fermion shadow (Class~C or~M assignment).
\end{itemize}


%% ------------------------------------------------------------------

\noindent
\emph{Status}: ten equivalences
(\ref{item:kp-def})--(\ref{item:kp-fmbdy}) proved unconditionally;
the Lagrangian criterion~(\ref{item:kp-lagrangian}) now
unconditional for the standard landscape
(Proposition~\ref{prop:lagrangian-perfectness} verifies
perfectness at non-critical, non-degenerate levels);
$\mathcal{D}$-module purity~(\ref{item:kp-dmod})
partially proved (forward direction, converse open).
Two further characterizations, tropical Koszulness
(Theorem~\ref{thm:tropical-koszulness}) and
bifunctor obstruction decomposition
(Theorem~\ref{thm:bifunctor-obstruction-decomposition}),
are proved separately but are not among the twelve numbered
conditions.

\smallskip\noindent
\emph{Proof circuit.}
The core cycle
(\ref{item:kp-def})$\Leftrightarrow$(\ref{item:kp-pbw})$\Leftrightarrow$(\ref{item:kp-ainfty})$\Leftrightarrow$(\ref{item:kp-barcobar})$\Leftrightarrow$(\ref{item:kp-hochschild})
is proved by PBW concentration~$\to$
bar-cobar inversion~$\to$ Hochschild polynomial growth~$\to$
Koszul-complex acyclicity, with $A_\infty$ formality equivalent
to PBW via Keller classicality.  From this core,
Ext diagonal vanishing~(\ref{item:kp-ext}) follows by bigrading
constraints,
Barr--Beck--Lurie~(\ref{item:kp-barrbeck}) by conservativity +
monadic descent (\cite[Prop.~4.7.3.16]{HA}),
FH concentration~(\ref{item:kp-facthom}) via bar = FH,
Kac--Shapovalov~(\ref{item:kp-nullvec}) via Shapovalov
non-degeneracy, FM boundary acyclicity~(\ref{item:kp-fmbdy})
by stratum-by-stratum PBW, and
the Lagrangian criterion~(\ref{item:kp-lagrangian}) via PTVV
derived-intersection theory (unconditional for the standard
landscape by Proposition~\ref{prop:lagrangian-perfectness}).


%% ====================================================================
%%  RECTIFICATION: THE ORGANIZING META-THEOREM
%% ====================================================================
\section{Rectification: the organizing meta-theorem}
\label{sec:concordance-rectification}
\index{rectification!organizing meta-theorem|textbf}
\index{formality!as universal mechanism|textbf}

Rectification, the passage from a homotopy-algebraic structure
to a strict one without loss of invariant data, is the single
mechanism underlying all five MC levels and the main conjectures
in the non-principal corridor.

\begin{center}
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.25}
\begin{tabular}{@{}llp{7.5cm}@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Level} & \textbf{Formality input} & \textbf{Consequence} \\
\midrule
MC1 & PBW filtration & Genus-$0$ bar complex is formal:
  $E_2$-degeneration gives $H^*(\barB(\cA)) \cong$ quadratic dual
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:pbw-koszulness-criterion}) \\
MC2 & $D^2 = 0$ & Bar-intrinsic MC element: $\Theta_\cA := D_\cA - d_0$
  is automatically MC because $D_\cA^2 = 0$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:mc2-bar-intrinsic}).
  No homotopy correction needed \\
MC3 & Prefundamental CG & \textbf{PROVED for all simple types}
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:categorical-cg-all-types},
  Corollary~\ref{cor:mc3-all-types}).
  Key input: multiplicity-free $q$-characters for fundamental reps
  \cite{ChariMoura06} replace the minuscule hypothesis.
  Type~$A$ proof (Theorem~\ref{thm:mc3-type-a-resolution})
  generalizes verbatim via $\ell$-weight block separation \\
MC4 & Strong filtration & Completion is formal inverse limit: the strong
  filtration axiom $\mu_r(F^{i_1},\ldots,F^{i_r}) \subset
  F^{i_1+\cdots+i_r}$ gives arity cutoff
  (Lemma~\ref{lem:arity-cutoff}), making continuity
  and Mittag-Leffler automatic
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:completed-bar-cobar-strong}) \\
MC5 & HS-sewing & Sewing = analytic continuation of the formal genus tower:
  polynomial OPE growth $+$ subexponential sector growth implies
  convergence at all genera
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:general-hs-sewing}) \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\begin{remark}[DS--KD filtration formality route]
\label{rem:ds-kd-formality-route}
\index{Drinfeld--Sokolov!$E_1$ degeneration route}
\index{BRST complex!filtration formality}
The DS--KD intertwining for non-principal
$\mathcal{W}$-algebras
(Conjecture~\ref{conj:ds-kd-arbitrary-nilpotent})
reduces to filtration formality ($E_1$ degeneration of the Kazhdan filtration spectral sequence) of the BRST complex.
The derived DS functor~$R\mathrm{DS}_f$ agrees with
$H^0_{Q_{\mathrm{DS}}}$ on Koszul algebras at generic level,
because the BRST complex is filtration-formal by the Kazhdan filtration
argument: the Kazhdan filtration on
$V_k(\fg) \otimes \mathcal{F}_{\mathfrak{n}_+}$ gives
$E_1$-degeneration at generic~$k$, and the resulting
$E_1$-page is the $\mathcal{W}$-algebra with no higher
corrections.  The obstruction to extending this beyond generic
level is the possible failure of $E_1$-degeneration at
rational~$k$ (admissible/critical levels), where vacuum null
vectors can produce genuine higher differentials.
The hook-type corridor is the first natural audit surface for this
route, but the manuscript currently contains incompatible summaries
of the type-$A$ abelian-$\mathfrak{n}_+$ locus, so the hook-wide
extension is not used as unconditional input.  Accordingly the
hook corridor remains conditional
(Theorem~\ref{thm:hook-transport-corridor}), and the
$(3,2)$-nilpotent in~$\mathfrak{sl}_5$ remains the first explicit
non-abelian case where the filtration-formality argument requires
genuine new work.
\end{remark}


%% ====================================================================
%%  NON-PRINCIPAL W-ALGEBRA DUALITY: THE TRANSPORT FRONTIER
%% ====================================================================
\section{Non-principal \texorpdfstring{$\mathcal{W}$}{W}-algebra
duality: the transport frontier}
\label{sec:concordance-non-principal-w}
\index{W-algebra@$\mathcal{W}$-algebra!non-principal duality!concordance}

After the principal Feigin--Frenkel case
(Theorem~\ref{thm:w-algebra-koszul-main}), the non-principal
duality problem splits into two axes
(Principle~\ref{princ:transport-orbit-factorization}):
\emph{transport along the reduction network} and
\emph{identification of the dual orbit/level}.

\paragraph{Proved core.}
\begin{itemize}
\item \emph{Principal}: Feigin--Frenkel duality, all simple~$\fg$.
\item \emph{Transport propagation}: duality propagates from hook
  vertices through the reduction graph~$\Gamma_N$ to every
  partition in the transport-closure
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:transport-propagation}).
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{Active frontier.}
\begin{itemize}
\item \emph{Subregular/minimal in $\mathfrak{sl}_3$}:
  explicit bar/OPE computations and strictness are proved, but the
  level-shifted Bershadsky--Polyakov duality statement remains
  conjectural
  (Conjecture~\ref{conj:bp-duality};
  Computation~\ref{comp:bp-bar};
  Theorem~\ref{thm:w-bp-strict}).
\item \emph{Hook-type corridor in type~$A$}:
  inverse reductions and transport data are available, but the full
  hook-type duality statement is kept conditional on hook-wide
  DS/bar compatibility
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:hook-transport-corridor}).
\item \emph{Type-$A$ transport-to-transpose}
  (Conjecture~\ref{conj:type-a-transport-to-transpose}):
  the transport-closure of the hook vertices equals
  $\mathrm{Par}(N)$ at generic level.
  Computationally verified for $N = 2, \ldots, 7$.
  The structural dividing line is
  $\mathfrak{n}_+$-abelianity: all hook-type orbits have abelian
  $\mathfrak{n}_+$, and the hook corridor covers exactly these.
  The partition $(3,2)$ in~$\mathfrak{sl}_5$ is the first
  genuine frontier case with non-abelian~$\mathfrak{n}_+$.
\item \emph{General orbit duality}
  (Conjecture~\ref{conj:w-orbit-duality}):
  extends to all simple~$\fg$ via Barbasch--Vogan/Spaltenstein
  duality.
\item \emph{DS--KD intertwining for arbitrary nilpotent}
  (Conjecture~\ref{conj:ds-kd-arbitrary-nilpotent}):
  bar--cobar duality commutes with DS reduction at arbitrary~$f$.
  The strongest route is via BRST formality
  (Remark~\ref{rem:ds-kd-formality-route}): the Kazhdan
  filtration gives a case-by-case route at abelian~$\mathfrak{n}_+$.
  Beyond that abelian locus, the formality of the BRST
  complex at rational~$k$ is the essential new input.
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{Hook-type quantitative data.}
\begin{itemize}
\item \emph{Ghost constant formula}
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:hook-ghost-constant}):
  $C_{(m,1^r)} = m(m^2-1)/6 + r\lfloor m^2/2\rfloor/2$.
  Verified for $\mathfrak{sl}_3$ through $\mathfrak{sl}_5$.
\item \emph{DS--bar commutation for hook-type}
  (Proposition~\ref{prop:ds-bar-hook-commutation}):
  kappa compatibility, generator matching, and central charge
  threading verified for all hook partitions in
  $\mathfrak{sl}_3$--$\mathfrak{sl}_5$.
\item \emph{Kappa sum rule}
  (Remark~\ref{rem:hook-kappa-sum-rule}):
  $\kappa(\mathcal{W}^k(f_\eta)) + \kappa(\mathcal{W}^{-k-2N}(f_{\eta^t}))
  = -(C_\eta + C_{\eta^t})$ is $k$-independent, automatic from
  linearity of ghost subtraction.
\item \emph{$\mathfrak{sl}_4$ data table}
  (Computation~\ref{comp:sl4-hook-data}): complete hook-type
  ghost constants, generator spectra, and centralizer dimensions.
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{$\mathcal{W}_3$ multi-variable shadow archetype.}
The $\mathcal{W}_3$ algebra is the first standard family requiring
the multi-variable shadow tower
(\S\ref{subsec:w3-shadow-archetype} in
Chapter~\ref{chap:w-algebras}).  Three independent quartic
channels appear: $\mathfrak{Q}_{TTTT}$, $\mathfrak{Q}_{TTWW}$,
and $\mathfrak{Q}_{WWWW}$, coupled by $\Lambda$-exchange
(cross-channel pole terms in $W$).  The denominator filtration
by $W$-charge
(Proposition~\ref{prop:w3-denominator-filtration}) organizes
these channels: each carries a factor
$(5c+22)^{-\lfloor q_W/2 \rfloor}$ from the Kac determinant
at spin-$3$ level.  The cubic correction
$\mathfrak{C}_{TWW} = d_W = 3$ (not $2$) reflects the
conformal weight of~$W$ and is fixed by the Jacobi identity
for the $T$-$W$-$W$ OPE.

\paragraph{Key constraint.}
The difficulty is \emph{not} the existence of quantum DS
reduction for arbitrary~$f$ (Kac--Roan--Wakimoto~\cite{KRW});
it is proving that bar--cobar/Koszul duality commutes with
arbitrary-nilpotent reduction, identifying the correct dual
nilpotent, and determining the non-principal level transform.

\paragraph{Geometric localization programme.}
\index{geometric localization!programme}
\index{Slodowy slice!localization programme}
The non-principal duality problem has a geometric reformulation
through the Slodowy-slice localization principle
(Remark~\ref{rem:ds-geometric-localization-principle},
Theorem~\ref{thm:master-commutative-square}).  The programme is:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\arabic*)},nosep]
\item \emph{Geometric localization theorem}
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:arakawa-variety-intersection},
  proved elsewhere): DS reduction at non-critical level =
  Hamiltonian reduction from $J_\infty(\fg^*)$ to $J_\infty(S_f)$
  (the arc space of the Slodowy slice).
\item \emph{Master commutative square}
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:master-commutative-square},
  proved here for principal $f$): the diagram connecting
  bar complexes, PBW filtrations, and Hamiltonian reduction
  commutes.  For arbitrary~$f$, the square is structural but the
  commutativity requires the non-principal PBW identification
  $\operatorname{gr}_F \mathcal{W}^k(\fg,f) \cong \bC[J_\infty(S_f)]$.
\item \emph{Barbasch--Vogan as Springer duality of Slodowy slices}
  (Remark~\ref{rem:bv-springer-duality}): orbit duality
  $f \leftrightarrow f^D$ has geometric content as duality of
  transverse slices under the Springer resolution; the curvature
  complementarity $\kappa + \kappa' = \mathrm{const}$ is an algebraic
  identity under the Feigin--Frenkel involution $t \mapsto -t$.
\item \emph{Shadow depth from Dirac bracket nonlinearity}
  (Remark~\ref{rem:ds-depth-increase-geometric}): the depth
  increase $L \to M$ under DS is the Taylor expansion of the
  nonlinear Dirac bracket on $J_\infty(S_f)$, created by
  Hamiltonian reduction from the linear Kirillov--Kostant bracket.
\item \emph{Holographic extension} (conjectural): the full
  holographic datum $H(T)$ should be functorial under DS-as-localization,
  with the boundary algebra localizing to $J_\infty(S_f)$ and the
  line category restricting accordingly.
\end{enumerate}
Items (1)--(4) are proved or structural; item~(5) is the conjectural
holographic lift.

\begin{remark}[Transport-closure and structural diagnostics]
\label{rem:transport-closure-diagnostics}
\index{transport-closure!Par(N) verification}
\index{kappa sum rule!non-hook orbits}
\index{W_N@$\mathcal{W}_N$!N-strict}
Computational verification yields four structural facts:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)},nosep]
\item \emph{Transport-closure $= \mathrm{Par}(N)$.}
  Verified for $N = 2, \ldots, 7$: the transport-closure
  of hook vertices in the reduction graph~$\Gamma_N$
  exhausts all partitions of~$N$.
\item \emph{$\mathfrak{n}_+$-abelianity as structural divide.}
  All hook-type orbits have abelian $\mathfrak{n}_+$;
  all non-hook orbits have non-abelian $\mathfrak{n}_+$.
  The Kazhdan formality argument extends exactly to the
  abelian locus.
\item \emph{Kappa sum constancy for non-hook orbits.}
  $\kappa(\mathcal{W}^k(\fg, f_\eta))
  + \kappa(\mathcal{W}^{-k-2h^\vee}(\fg, f_{\eta^t}))$
  is $k$-independent for all orbits, not only hook-type.
  This is automatic from linearity of the ghost subtraction,
  but the explicit value is non-trivial for non-hook orbits.
\item \emph{$\mathcal{W}_N$ is $N$-strict.}
  The Miura embedding gives $r_{\max}(\mathcal{W}_N) = \infty$
  for all $N \geq 2$ (shadow class~$\mathsf{M}$),
  verified through $N = 20$.
\end{enumerate}
\end{remark}


%% ====================================================================
%%  E1 MODULAR THEORY
%% ====================================================================
\section{\texorpdfstring{$E_1$}{E1} modular theory:
the ordered bar complex at all genera}
\label{sec:concordance-e1-modular-theory}
\index{E1 algebra@$E_1$-algebra!concordance|textbf}
\index{five main theorems!E1@$E_1$ variant!concordance}
\index{FAss@$F\Ass$!concordance}

The $E_\infty$ modular theory (Theorems~A--D+H, the shadow
Postnikov tower, $\Theta_\cA \in \mathrm{MC}(\gAmod)$) has an
$E_1$ counterpart in which symmetry is replaced by ordering.
The $E_1$ theory is developed as a standalone chapter
(Chapter~\ref{chap:e1-modular-koszul}), making the $E_1/E_\infty$
parallelism architecturally visible.
The following table records the parallel construction.

\begin{center}
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.15}
\begin{tabular}{lcc}
\toprule
\emph{Object}
  & \emph{$E_\infty$ \textup{(}symmetric\textup{)}}
  & \emph{$E_1$ \textup{(}ordered\textup{)}} \\
\midrule
Modular operad
  & $\cM_{\Com}$: $\overline{\cM}_{g,n}$
  & $\cM_{\Ass}$: $\overline{\cM}_{g,n}^{\mathrm{rib}}$
    \\
Feynman transform
  & $F\!\Com$
  & $F\!\Ass$ (Def.~\ref{def:feynman-transform-ass})
    \\
Convolution
  & $\gAmod$ (Def.~\ref{def:modular-convolution-dg-lie})
  & ${\gAmod}^{E_1}$ (Def.~\ref{def:e1-modular-convolution})
    \\
MC element
  & $\Theta_\cA = D_\cA - \dzero$
  & $\Theta_\cA^{E_1} = D_\cA^{E_1} - \dzero$
    \\
Arity-$2$ shadow
  & $\kappa(\cA)$ (scalar)
  & $r(z)$ ($R$-matrix)
    \\
Arity-$3$ shadow
  & $\mathfrak{C}(\cA)$ (cubic)
  & $r_3(z_1,z_2)$ (KZ associator)
    \\
Planted forests
  & $\mathbb{G}_{\mathrm{pf}}$ (unordered)
  & $\mathbb{G}_{\mathrm{pf}}^{\mathrm{pl}}$ (planar,
    Def.~\ref{def:planar-planted-forest-coefficient-algebra})
    \\
Ambient algebra
  & $\mathfrak{g}^{\mathrm{amb}}_\cA$
  & $\mathfrak{g}^{\mathrm{amb},E_1}_\cA$
    (Def.~\ref{def:ordered-ambient-algebra})
    \\
Coinvariant map
  & \multicolumn{2}{c}{%
    $\operatorname{av}\colon
    {\gAmod}^{E_1} \twoheadrightarrow \gAmod$;
    \quad $\operatorname{av}(\Theta^{E_1}) = \Theta$}
    \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\paragraph{Status of the $E_1$ five main theorems.}
\begin{center}
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.15}
\begin{tabular}{lccc}
\toprule
& \emph{Genus $0$} & \emph{All genera} & \emph{Reference} \\
\midrule
$\mathbf{A}^{E_1}$: bar--cobar
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & Thms~\ref{thm:e1-theorem-A},
    \ref{thm:e1-theorem-A-modular} \\
$\mathbf{B}^{E_1}$: inversion
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & Thms~\ref{thm:e1-theorem-B},
    \ref{thm:e1-theorem-B-modular} \\
$\mathbf{C}^{E_1}$: complementarity
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & Thms~\ref{thm:e1-theorem-C},
    \ref{thm:e1-theorem-C-modular} \\
$\mathbf{D}^{E_1}$: $R$-matrix
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & \textbf{Proved}

    \ref{thm:e1-theorem-D-modular} \\

  & \textbf{Proved}
  & \textbf{Proved}
  & Thms~\ref{thm:e1-theorem-H},
    \ref{thm:e1-theorem-H-modular} \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\paragraph{Resolved conjectures.}
\begin{itemize}
\item Ordered-associative modular Maurer--Cartan theory:
  Theorem~\ref{thm:ordered-associative-modular-mc} records the
  Volume~II resolution of the original modular conjecture.
  The $E_1$ modular convolution ${\gAmod}^{E_1}$ carries
  $\Theta_\cA^{E_1}$ by the bar-intrinsic construction.
\item Principal ordered-associative DS compatibility:
  Theorem~\ref{thm:ordered-associative-ds-principal} records the
  Volume~II principal-case theorem for DS reduction at non-critical level.
  Hook-type in type~$A$ also covered.
\item \texttt{conj:FG-shadow}: resolved at arities $2, 3, 4$
  (Theorem~\ref{thm:e1-coinvariant-shadow}).
  The $E_\infty$ shadow IS the $\Sigma_r$-coinvariant of
  the $E_1$ shadow.
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{Remaining conjectural frontier.}
\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{conj:FG-shadow} at all arities: the full
  abelianisation spectral sequence from
  ${\Barch}^{\mathrm{ord}}$ to $\Barch$ requires analysis at
  infinite arity.
\item \texttt{conj:bordered}: geometric realisation of the
  diagonal bicomodule via bordered ordered configuration
  spaces.  \emph{Partially resolved}: items~(1)--(3) and~(5) follow
  from the bordered FM compactification of
  \S\ref{sec:bordered-fm}
  (Construction~\ref{constr:bordered-fm},
  Theorem~\ref{thm:bordered-fm-properties}).  Item~(4) (annular
  closure) remains conjectural, pending the annular bordered FM
  compactification.
\item Conjecture~\ref{conj:DS-arbitrary-nilpotent} for arbitrary
  nilpotent $f$: requires
  Koszul-BRST commutation for non-principal reduction.
\end{itemize}


\section{Structural upgrades}
\label{sec:concordance-structural-upgrades}

\paragraph{Shadow archetype classification and single-line dichotomy.}
Theorem~\ref{thm:shadow-archetype-classification} classifies the
standard-landscape shadow depth classes
($\mathbf{G}$/$\mathbf{L}$/$\mathbf{C}$/$\mathbf{M}$
$= \mathbf{F}_2/\mathbf{F}_3/\mathbf{F}_4/\mathbf{M}$)
with complete proofs for all primitive archetypes.
Shadow depth is orthogonal
to Koszulness: all computed archetypes are chirally Koszul, yet their
shadow depths differ.
The single-line dichotomy
(Theorem~\ref{thm:single-line-dichotomy}) proves the gap between
$\mathbf{F}_4$ and $\mathbf{M}$ is structural, not empirical:
on any one-dimensional primary slice of
$\Defcyc^{\mathrm{mod}}(\cA)$, every shadow coefficient
$S_r$ ($r \geq 4$) factors through the critical discriminant
$\Delta = 8\kappa S_4$, and the quotients $R_r = S_r/\Delta$
are generically nonvanishing, so $r_{\max} \in \{2, 3, \infty\}$
on any single line.  The contact class $\mathbf{C}$ escapes to
$r_{\max} = 4$ via stratum separation
(Remark~\ref{rem:contact-stratum-separation}):
the quartic contact invariant lives on a charged stratum
of $\Defcyc^{\mathrm{mod}}$ whose self-bracket
exits the complex by rank-one abelian rigidity.
The algebraic depth $d_{\mathrm{alg}} \in \{0, 1, 2, \infty\}$
(Remark~\ref{rem:contact-stratum-separation}).
Depths $d \geq 5$ in the decomposition
$d = 1 + d_{\mathrm{arith}} + d_{\mathrm{alg}}$
(Theorem~\ref{thm:depth-decomposition})
are purely arithmetic.

\paragraph{Non-simply-laced Kac--Moody shadow verification.}
The shadow tower computation extends to all non-simply-laced
Kac--Moody algebras: $B_2 = \mathfrak{so}(5)$, $C_2 = \mathfrak{sp}(4)$,
$G_2$, $B_3 = \mathfrak{so}(7)$, and $F_4$.
All are class~$\mathbf{L}$ (depth~$3$): $S_3 = 1$, $S_4 = 0$,
$\Delta = 0$, independent of type and rank.  The distinction
$h \neq h^\vee$ for non-simply-laced types (e.g.\ $B_2$: $h = 4$,
$h^\vee = 3$; $G_2$: $h = 6$, $h^\vee = 4$) affects the bar-cohomology
periodicity (period $= 2h$, \emph{not}~$2h^\vee$) but not the
shadow depth class.  Bar $H^1 = \dim(\mathfrak{g})$ in all cases
(10 for~$B_2$, 10 for~$C_2$, 14 for~$G_2$).
Langlands duality $B_2 \leftrightarrow C_2$ preserves
$\kappa$ at the same level, confirmed computationally.

\paragraph{Minimal model shadow towers.}
Since minimal models $M(p,q)$ are simple quotients of the
Virasoro algebra, their shadow tower at the universal level
coincides with the Virasoro tower at $c = c(M(p,q))$:
class~$\mathbf{M}$ with the standard shadow metric.
At the quotient level, the curved-DG structure introduces
curvature at the degree of the first null vector (level~$pq$
for~$M(p,q)$).  The modular $S$-matrix and Verlinde fusion
rules are verified computationally for $M(4,3)$ (Ising, $c = 1/2$),
$M(5,4)$ (tricritical Ising, $c = 7/10$),
and $M(6,5)$ (three-state Potts, $c = 4/5$).
The shadow metric
$Q_L(t) = (2\kappa + 3\alpha t)^2 + 2\Delta\,t^2$
(Definition~\ref{def:shadow-metric}) packages the dichotomy
geometrically: $Q_L$ is a perfect square iff
$\Delta = 0$, and the spectral curve
$\Sigma_L = \{H^2 = t^4 Q_L\}$
(Corollary~\ref{cor:spectral-curve}) is rational.

\paragraph{Ran-coherent bar-cobar equivalence.}
Theorem~\ref{thm:ran-coherent-bar-cobar} resolves the Ran-space
formality gap identified in earlier audits: the bar-cobar
quasi-isomorphism extends coherently from
$\operatorname{Ran}^{\leq n}(X)$ to all of
$\operatorname{Ran}(X)$ via the strong completion-tower theorem
and the arity cutoff lemma.

\paragraph{Ambient complementarity FMP upgrade.}
Theorem~\ref{thm:ambient-complementarity-fmp} is upgraded from
\texttt{Conjectured} to \texttt{ProvedHere}: the modular cyclic
deformation complex $\Defcyc^{\mathrm{mod}}(\cA)$ is already a
complete filtered cyclic dg~Lie algebra, and the Lurie--Pridham
correspondence + PTVV theorem give the $(-1)$-shifted symplectic
formal moduli problem with Lagrangian maps unconditionally (under
the standing perfectness/nondegeneracy hypotheses).

\paragraph{Chiral Deligne--Tamarkin principle and the dimensional jump.}
Remark~\ref{rem:chiral-deligne-tamarkin-dimensional-jump} makes
explicit the mechanism by which every local $A_\infty$-chiral algebra
on a curve produces a local $3$-dimensional holomorphic-topological
bulk/boundary system: the chiral center theorem
(Theorem~\ref{thm:operadic-center-hochschild}) provides the
universal closed-sector algebra
$C^\bullet_{\mathrm{ch}}(\cA,\cA)$ acting on~$\cA$ through
$\SCchtop$, and the recognition theorem (Volume~II, items F4--F5)
identifies the resulting pair with a local HT prefactorization
algebra on $D \times \bR$.  The extra dimension is the universal
normal-collar direction of a codimension-one boundary condition,
forced by the center construction.  The physical realization is the
Khan--Zeng PVA-to-3d-HT construction~\cite{KhanZeng25}
(Proposition~\ref{prop:pva-degree-constraint}): gauge invariance
$\Leftrightarrow$ $\lambda$-Jacobi identity; inner Virasoro element
$\Rightarrow$ full topological symmetry.

\paragraph{Modular trace principle.}
Principle~\ref{princ:modular-trace} (Volume~II) organizes the modular
structure as trace-plus-clutching on the open factorization
category~$\cC$.  Three of its four ingredients are proved: (i)~cyclic
structure (Calabi--Yau on $\cC(J)$), (ii)~annulus identification
$\int_{S^1_p} \cC \simeq \HH_\bullet(A_b)$
(Theorem~\ref{thm:vol2-annulus-trace}), and (iii)~the closed-sector
modular MC equation for~$\Theta_\cA$
(Volume~I, Theorem~\ref{thm:mc2-bar-intrinsic}).  The fourth
ingredient (the full open-sector modular twisting morphism extending
to the bordered log-modular cooperad) is conjectural and constitutes
the global factorization descent problem.

\paragraph{Quartic logarithmic contact class.}
Definition~\ref{def:quartic-log-contact-class} (Volume~II) defines
$\mathfrak{q}_4(\cA) \in H^2(\gr_4\,\Conv^{\mathrm{mod},\leq 4})$,
the first logarithmic modular obstruction from codimension-$2$
log-Fulton--MacPherson strata at arity~$4$.
Proposition~\ref{prop:quartic-contact-vanishes-BL} proves
$\mathfrak{q}_4 = 0$ in the boundary-linear LG sector (by strict
commutativity and associativity); for Virasoro and $\cW_3$,
$\mathfrak{q}_4 \neq 0$ (Volume~I shadow tower computations),
distinguishing shadow depth class~$\mathbf{M}$ from~$\mathbf{G}/\mathbf{L}/\mathbf{C}$.

\paragraph{Shadow separation
\textup{(}Theorem~\textup{\ref{thm:shadow-separation}}\textup{)}.}
$\Theta_\cA = \varprojlim \Theta_\cA^{\leq r}$ in
$\widehat{\gAmod}$; gauge-equivalent MC classes have
identical shadow towers.  Separating witnesses:
$\kappa(\cH_1) = \kappa(\mathrm{Vir}_2)$ but
$\mathfrak{C}_{\cH} = 0 \neq \mathfrak{C}_{\mathrm{Vir}}$
(level~$3$);
$(\kappa, \mathfrak{C})_{\cH_0}
= (\kappa, \mathfrak{C})_{\beta\gamma}$ but
$\mathfrak{Q}_{\cH_0} = 0 \neq
\mathfrak{Q}_{\beta\gamma}$ (level~$4$).
Shadow class detected by the vanishing pattern
$(\mathrm{Sh}_3, \mathrm{Sh}_4, \mathrm{Sh}_5)$.
$r_{\max}(\cA^!) = r_{\max}(\cA)$
(Corollary~\ref{cor:shadow-depth-koszul-invariance}).

\paragraph{Shadow tautological classes
\textup{(}Theorem~\textup{\ref{thm:shadow-tautological-ring}}\textup{)}.}
